# Page

- **Name**: Frequently Asked Questions | Alpha School
- **URL**: https://alpha.school/faq/
- **Description**: Find answers to common questions about Alpha School. Learn more about our programs, admissions, and unique approach to education.

Frequently Asked Questions
==========================

   TOPICS

- The Alpha Learning Model
- Academics, Progress &amp; Results
- AI, Technology &amp; Guides
- Social Development, Life Skills &amp; Enrichment
- Enrollment, Tuition &amp; Logistics

    The Alpha Learning Model

  Are kids only in school for 2 hours?    No. Students attend a full school day, similar to a traditional school schedule.

The difference is that core academics are completed in about two hours using personalized, mastery-based learning software. By condensing academics into two hours, students move faster than in a traditional classroom while achieving deep mastery of the material.

The rest of the day is intentionally designed for activities that traditional schools often struggle to fit in, including:

● Leadership workshops
● Public speaking
● Entrepreneurship projects
● Team collaboration
● Physical activity
● Creative problem solving
● Life skills development

This model is often referred to as “2-Hour Learning.” It allows students to complete rigorous academics efficiently while gaining practical, real-world skills.

  Do students sit on computers all day?    No.

Students typically spend about two hours per day on academic learning software. The remainder of the school day includes interactive and collaborative experiences such as:

● Group projects
● Socratic discussions
● Leadership challenges
● Entrepreneurship labs
● Public speaking workshops
● Physical activity
● Creative exploration

The goal is to use technology only where it improves learning, and dedicate the rest of the day to human interaction and skill development.

  Why does Alpha School focus on completing academics efficiently?    The goal is not to reduce academic rigor. Instead, the goal is to remove inefficiencies from the traditional classroom model.

In traditional schools, much of the day is spent on lectures, waiting for classmates to catch up, or repeating material students already understand.

Personalized learning allows students to:

● Move forward once they master a concept
● Spend more time where they need support
● Progress faster in subjects where they excel

This efficiency frees up time for leadership development and life skills.

  What are examples of Alpha’s motivational models?    Alpha’s motivational models are both individualized and collective. Guides are responsible for understanding and knowing what motivates each individual student and designing collective rewards when students meet their goals. The guides also ensure that students understand the logic behind the motivation model, ultimately making children self-driven. Students can earn time outside, or in the Alpha “ThinkTank” room, or earn “Alphas”, our school currency that they can use to purchase prizes or larger rewards such as a laser tag party.

   Academics, Progress &amp; Results

  Do students still learn core subjects like math, reading, and science?    Yes.

Students complete all state and federal mandated core curriculum covering all academic subjects, including:

● Mathematics
● Reading and writing
● Science
● History and social studies

The difference is that students progress through the material using mastery-based learning, meaning they only move forward once they fully understand the concept.

  Does my child have access to school work or content above their level?    There is no ceiling for academic progression so students are able to progress at their own pace. Alpha champions unrestricted academic progression. Students aren’t confined by traditional grade levels; a 2nd grader ready for 5th-grade math will engage with that level, ensuring a truly personalized learning journey and harnessing of potential.

  Is the Alpha School model proven?    Alpha School has been operating for more than a decade and continues to expand as families seek alternatives to traditional education models.

Students regularly take nationally recognized assessments such as MAP Growth, which allow progress to be measured against national benchmarks.

Results have consistently shown that Alpha students perform in the top 1–2% nationally and frequently progress academically twice as fast as the national average.

  Is the Alpha model new or experimental?    Alpha School has been operating for more than a decade and has expanded to multiple campuses across the United States.

The model has been refined over years of classroom experience and is supported by research on mastery learning, adaptive software, and personalized education.

  Is Alpha School an experiment?    Alpha School is the result of more than a decade of development and iteration.

The model combines well-established educational principles such as:

● Mastery-based learning
● Personalized instruction
● Mentorship-based teaching
● Project-based learning

These ideas have been studied for decades and are combined at Alpha, in collaboration with some of the world’s leading learning scientists, in a way that allows students to learn efficiently while developing real-world skills.

   AI, Technology &amp; Guides

  Is a robot teaching the students?    No. There is no robot teaching students at Alpha School.

While students use personalized learning software to complete their academic lessons, that technology is simply a tool, not a robot. Using this AI-tutor means:

● Every student learns at the right level for them
● Students can move faster in subjects they excel in
● Students receive additional practice when needed
● Students achieve 90% mastery in each concept before they move on

Students at Alpha spend more meaningful time with caring adults than in traditional schools. The heart of Alpha is the Guide, not the technology.

Guides are dedicated mentors who work closely with students each day. They don’t stand at the front of a classroom delivering lectures. Instead, they spend their time coaching, motivating, and truly getting to know each child.

At Alpha, the standard for Guides is to have a deep impact on every student. Guides make the learning meaningful. They focus on building trust, developing confidence, and helping every student grow, not just academically, but as a person.

  Is AI replacing teachers?    No. Alpha School believes great educators are more important than ever.

The difference is how their time is used.

Instead of spending most of the day delivering lectures and grading assignments, Alpha Guides focus on mentorship, coaching, and helping students develop confidence, resilience, and leadership skills.

In fact, Alpha School invests heavily in its educators. Guides earn six-figure salaries, reflecting the importance of their role in student development.

  Does Alpha School really have no teachers?    Alpha School absolutely has educators.

At Alpha, the role of the teacher is redefined and elevated. Instead of lecturing the same lesson to 25–30 students at once, our educators, called Guides, focus on what humans do best:

● Mentoring students
● Supporting emotional development
● Coaching leadership skills
● Encouraging curiosity and motivation
● Helping students set and achieve goals

Because AI and adaptive software handle routine academic instruction, Guides can spend more time supporting each student individually.

  How does Alpha select Guides?    We take deep pride in hiring at Alpha. Guides are selected based on: 1) their ability to motivate and know students, 2) their ability to plan engaging life skills workshops. And 3) their affinity to understanding what the student requires in terms of support. We select Guides from top universities across the country with competitive backgrounds in fields like tech and start-ups. Alpha Guides are not just supervisors or teachers – they are much more than that!

   Social Development, Life Skills &amp; Enrichment

  Does app-based learning mean less social interaction?    Not at all! While students spend 2 hours on apps in the morning, the rest of their day is spent in engaging with their peers and getting direction from the guides via an array of lively activities. In fact, because they don’t have to spend 6 hours looking in the same direction at a chalkboard, Alpha students get more socialization than the average school student.

  Do students still interact with other students in the Alpha model?    Yes. Alpha students collaborate frequently throughout the day.

Because academics are completed efficiently, students actually have more time for collaboration and group activities than in traditional school models.

Students regularly participate in:

● Team projects
● Leadership challenges
● Public speaking exercises
● Socratic discussions
● Clubs and extracurricular activities

  How does Alpha School support students socially?    Alpha students spend much of the day working together on challenges, discussions, and projects.

Because academics are completed efficiently, students actually have more time for collaboration and social interaction than in traditional schools.

Students regularly participate in:

● Team challenges
● Public speaking events
● Group projects
● Leadership exercises
● Clubs and activities

  Who is Alpha School designed for?    Alpha School is designed for students who thrive when they can learn at their own pace and develop real-world skills alongside strong academics.

Families are often drawn to Alpha because it offers:

● Personalized learning
● Leadership development
● Entrepreneurial thinking
● A future-focused education model

  Why does Alpha School focus on life skills?    Traditional education often prioritizes memorization and standardized testing. Alpha School believes students should also develop skills that matter in the real world.

That includes:

● Leadership
● Communication
● Entrepreneurship
● Critical thinking
● Resilience
● Collaboration

These skills are intentionally built into the school day and led by Guides.

  What are examples of workshops at Alpha?    Alpha believes that students need enrichment and exposure to a variety of spheres, and we have thus hosted workshops of several types. We continue to design and host content that students love. Workshops have included topics such as Alpha Mad Scientists (life skill: learn to learn), Alpha Animation Studios (public speaking and storytelling), Lyrical Genius (brand building), Consultants (be an expert), How to Buy Stuff (personal finance), Now You See Me (public speaking and storytelling), among many others.

   Enrollment, Tuition &amp; Logistics

  What grade levels does Alpha serve?    It depends on the [location](/locations/). For example, Alpha Austin is a preK-12 school. Alpha works in levels that are based on specific capabilities as opposed to traditional grade models. Age is not the deciding factor of acumen, and we put that into practice.

  Is Alpha School an online school?    We have both. Alpha School is an in-person school with a full campus experience.

Students attend school together each day, collaborate on projects, participate in workshops, and build friendships just like in a traditional school setting.

Alpha Anywhere is the online version of Alpha School, which is mostly used by homeschoolers. It is the same academic platform that students use at Alpha School, completing academics in just two hours per day.

  What's included in the tuition?    Alpha tuition is inclusive of ALL student activities (like a trip to Formula 1 or Poland); Alpha will never EVER ask parents for additional fundraising. With this in mind, Alpha tuition remains on par with the nation’s best private schools.

  When will Alpha School be coming to my city?    Alpha School is expanding to new cities across the United States as demand grows. Families who are interested in bringing Alpha to their area can register their interest here:

[**https://alpha.school/bring-alpha-to-your-city/**](https://alpha.school/bring-alpha-to-your-city/)

When you complete the interest form, our team tracks demand by city and region. The best way to accelerate Alpha coming to your area is to raise your hand and let us know you’re interested. Families who submit the form will be the first to receive updates if we begin exploring a campus in their city.

  How do I request a transcript or test scores?    Just email our registrar at <registrar@alpha.school>, and they’ll be happy to help!

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha Austin serve?**: Alpha Austin is located in Barton Hills on Spyglass Dr. serving families throughout the Austin Metropolitan area. Our community spans Travis and Hayes county. If that includes you, we’d be excited to deliver an innovative and personalized education for your children.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We explored many spaces across Austin, and this one stood out. It offered the right blend of flexibility, safety, design potential, and proximity to the entire Austin metro and MoPac, offering easy access from all Austin neighborhoods.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes at least 1 hour and 15 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting, where sudents take advantage of our playground and large outdoor space. In addition to free play, many of our life skills workshops include outdoor time either on site or at nearby destinations like miniature golf or tennis facilities, horse stables, local pools, and more! Fresh air, sunshine, and active movement are built into our day!
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress, ensuring mastery of each topic. This allows each Austin student to master core academic subjects at their own pace—with no gaps, no burnout, and consistent 1:1 support.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and also master life goals in each workshop—from running a business to running a 5K. Whether a student lives downtown, in Cedar Park, or South Austin, they’re on a path that fits them perfectly.
- **Is Alpha Austin open?**: Yes, Alpha Austin is enrolling for PreK–8. Now in year 11 and with more than 150 students, we continue to actively grow. So, if you’d like to tour the campus or connect with a current family, we’d love to show you around.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in Plano​
--------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Plano, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Plano, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Plano is open and enrolling.

Join us for an info session at our campus on 7220 Independence Pkwy, and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Tasha Arnold](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha Schools because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>   - Dr Tasha Arnold

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Screenshot-2026-04-30-124548.webp) 

Andy Gibson | Dean of Parents of Alpha School in Plano
------------------------------------------------------

Andy Gibson has dedicated his career to youth development through sport and education. He has worked with the Dallas Stars and USA Hockey to grow ice hockey and founded Dallas Stars Adaptive Sports to create inclusive opportunities for all athletes. A former U.S. Peace Corps volunteer, he’s passionate about helping kids reach their full potential.

> A ship in harbor is safe, but that is not what ships are built for.
> 
>  - John A. Shedd

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/10/Jennifer-Maddox.jpg) 

Jennifer Maddox | Lead Guide
----------------------------

With 20 years in education, Jennifer is thrilled to be part of the Alpha community! She’s served as an elementary teacher, academic coach, and education specialist with Kentucky’s Department of Education. As a National Board Certified Teacher with training in Orton Gillingham and LETRS, she’s passionate about literacy and helping every student reach their fullest potential.

> My goal is to create an environment where every child loves coming to school, where curiosity drives learning, growth feels exciting, and students not only master academics but build life skills that shape driven, confident learners!
> 
>  - Jennifer Maddox

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Whitney Bunn](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Whitneys-Headshot.webp) 

Whitney Bunn | Guide
--------------------

Whitney has spent six years teaching math, writing curriculum, and leading students to the highest academic growth in her district. She has also built successful businesses, from a clothing brand to a chatbot service to managing rentals. Her greatest passion is helping kids see how capable, creative, and powerful they are.

> I bring contagious enthusiasm, keep learning in the “just right” challenge zone, and connect lessons to what makes each student tick so they grow fast and believe in themselves.
> 
>  - Whitney Bunn

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/10/Sanura-Njaka.png) 

Sanura N'Jaka | Guide
---------------------

Sanura brings a thoughtful, human-centered approach to her role as a Guide at Alpha. With experience teaching abroad, coaching underprivileged youth, and running a life coaching practice, she helps students connect deeply with themselves and others. Her background in psychology and technology shapes her unique, reflective approach to problem-solving and learning.

> Learning thrives when kids feel safe to be curious and authentic. I guide students to know themselves, think critically, and grow the emotional intelligence to live with confidence.
> 
>  - Sanura N'Jaka

Welcome to the Future of Education in Fort Worth​
-------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Fort Worth, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Fort Worth, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Fort Worth is open and enrolling.

Join us for an info session at our campus, 3300 Bryant Irvin Rd, conveniently located within the CERA recreational facility, just south of the Trinity River crossing and west of the Clearfork shopping center. See firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

### Campus

- **Alpha Fort Worth (https://alpha.school/fort-worth/)**
  - **Email**: admissions.fortworth@alpha.school
  - **Telephone**: +18173309327
  - **Address**: 3300 Bryant Irvin Rd, Fort Worth, Texas, 76109, US
  - **Geo**: 32.7021888, -97.41356189999999

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha Fort Worth serve?**: Alpha Fort Worth is located on Bryant Irvin Rd at the CERA facility just south of the Trinity River crossing, west of the Clearfork shopping center. We serve families from many areas in Fort Worth and Dallas—Aledo, Tanglewood, Ridglea, Arbor Lawn, Crowley, Arlington, Keller, Southlake, Colleyville, Richardson, Highland Park and other DFW areas. If you live near any of these ZIP codes 76107, 76109, 76110, 76248, 76034, 75081, 75205, among others, Alpha Fort Worth delivers an innovative and personalized education for your children.
- **Do you provide transportation?**: At this time, Alpha Fort Worth does not offer a formal transportation service. However, distance hasn’t stopped families from joining our community! Many coordinate carpools, and we actively help connect parents who live near one another. As our community grows, we’re exploring ways to expand transportation options so families across the metroplex can access Alpha’s unique model.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60–90 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting. They also have access to the racquetball courts, expansive fields, and large indoor gymnasium within the CERA center for free play as well as for structured activities. Students also often enjoy movement-based games and activities in nearby green spaces like River Park and Trinity Trails. Our location also takes advantage of proximity to destinations like the award-winning Fort Worth Zoo, the Stockyards, the Water Gardens, facilities at nearby Texas Christian University, and more! Fresh air and sunshine are built into our day!
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Our Fort Worth students are mastering core subjects at their own pace—with no gaps, no burnout, and no unnecessary review.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and choose exciting workshops—anything from aviation to zoology—based on their unique interests! Whether a student lives in Aledo or Southlake, they’re on a path that fits them perfectly.
- **Is Alpha Fort Worth open?**: Yes, Alpha Fort Worth is open and enrolling for K–8. Since we launched in Fall 2025, we’ve been actively growing. So, if you’d like to tour the campus or connect with a current family, we’d love to show you around.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in Scottsdale​
-------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Scottsdale, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Scottsdale, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Scottsdale is open and enrolling.

Join us for an info session at our campus on 20624 N. 76th St., next to Greyhawk Park, and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Tasha Arnold](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha Schools because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>   - Dr Tasha Arnold

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Screenshot-2026-04-30-123218.webp) 

Dr. Crystle Dorsey | Dean of Parents of Alpha School in Scottsdale
------------------------------------------------------------------

Crystle is an experienced educator and senior administrator with over 18 years in higher education focused on student success, leadership development and engagement. She holds a Ph.D. from the University of New Mexico where her teaching and research focuses on identity development.

> I came to Alpha as a prospective parent — working here has made me a better one. Watching families grow alongside their kids has been truly inspiring.
> 
>  - Crystle Dorsey

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/850A0037-scaled-1-801x1024.jpg) 

Zac DeJovine | Guide
--------------------

Zac has taught geometry, Spanish, science, and math, and spent years tutoring one-on-one to turn challenges into triumphs. He earned a full-tuition scholarship to ASU and a Master’s in Sustainable Food Systems. As a 6–8 Guide at Alpha Scottsdale, he fosters growth mindsets and shows every student they’re capable of more than they imagined.

> Relationship-building is the cornerstone of student success. When kids feel valued, they’re willing to take risks and achieve more than even they think possible.
> 
>  - Zac DeJovine

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/850A9986-1-scaled-1-828x1024.jpg) 

Matt Shenker | Lead Guide
-------------------------

Matt is an educator, licensed therapist, and behavior strategist who’s spent over a decade innovating how people learn. He’s built AI coaching tools, led global workplace training programs, and worked with thousands of young people to upgrade their skills for navigating life. As Lead Guide at Alpha Scottsdale, he’s building one of the greatest schools in the world.

> Motivation isn’t something kids either have or don’t. It’s something their environment either builds or breaks.
> 
>  - Matt Shenker

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/850A0263-2-scaled-1-1024x993.jpg) 

Holly Haygood | Reading Specialist
----------------------------------

For a decade, Holly has helped students surprise themselves with what they can achieve—leading literacy and inclusion programs, creating personalized learning plans, and bringing hands-on experiences to life. As a Reading Specialist and Alpha Guide in Scottsdale, she helps students build advanced skills and confidence, proving nothing is impossible with the right support.

> Kids can achieve incredible things when their adults refuse to accept mediocrity. I believe in seeing the infinite potential in each student before they see it in themselves.
> 
>  - Holly Haygood

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/unnamed-2-1024x1024.webp) 

Patricio Rosas | Guide
----------------------

Patricio holds an MBA in Leadership Development and has an extensive background coaching youth and college athletes, including serving as Head Coach for Phoenix Rising’s U15 girls team and Assistant Coach for both the men’s and women’s programs at Glendale Community College. He has also served as a Dean of Families, bringing experience supporting student growth both on and off the field, and is a licensed EMT. Most importantly, Patricio is a passionate mentor who believes deeply in high standards paired with high support and in helping students unlock potential they often don’t see in themselves. Outside of work Patricio enjoys spending time with his family, hiking, and working out. He likes reading, going to the movies, and pushing himself to learn new skills

> I hold high standards and build strong relationships so students gain confidence, take ownership, and never back away from a challenge.
> 
>  - Patricio Rosas

### Campus

- **Alpha Scottsdale (https://alpha.school/scottsdale/)**
  - **Email**: admissions.scottsdale@alpha.school

  - **Address**: 20624 N 76th St, Scottsdale, Arizona, 85255, US
  - **Geo**: 33.6729686, -111.9166703

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha Scottsdale serve?**: Alpha Scottsdale is located just off N 76th Street in North Scottsdale, serving families from Grayhawk, DC Ranch, McDowell Mountain Ranch, Pinnacle Peak, Troon, Paradise Valley, Kierland, Ancala, and nearby neighborhoods. Families living in ZIP codes 85255, 85260, 85262, and 85254 will find our school especially convenient. Whether you’re coming from Kierland Commons, WestWorld, OldTown, or the Scottsdale Airpark area, Alpha Scottsdale provides an innovative and personalized education within minutes of home.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We explored many spaces across Scottsdale and Paradise Valley, and this one stood out. It offered the right blend of safety, open space, and design potential. The campus is minutes from the Loop 101 for easy Valley-wide access and surrounded by family-friendly hubs like the Music Instrument Museum, Kierland Commons, Scottsdale Quarter, and McDowell Sonoran Preserve. It’s the perfect setting for a school that balances academic focus with outdoor exploration and community connection.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60–90 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting. Our Scottsdale campus has a full basketball court, three playground structures, a gaga pit, and an open green field the size of a football field—perfect for movement games, biking, and team sports. We also take advantage of nearby outdoor destinations like McDowell Sonoran Preserve, Pinnacle Peak Park, Camelback Mountain, and Scottsdale’s many community parks. From desert hikes to wide-open play, fresh air and sunshine are built into every student’s day!
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in San Francisco​
----------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha San Francisco, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha San Francisco, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha San Francisco is open and enrolling.

Join us for an info session at 3741 Buchanan St. in the Marina District and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Tasha Arnold](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha Schools because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>  - Dr. Tasha Arnold

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/ALPHA_PICDAY_1225-2-1024x803.jpg) 

Carson Lehmann | Lead Guide
---------------------------

Carson is a visionary leader who sparks students’ passion for learning and growth. Starting as a 3rd–4th grade Guide at Alpha Austin, he quickly stood out for personalizing learning and building confidence. From coding drones to LSAT logic puzzles to Wharton simulations, he pushes students to exceed expectations. Blending heart and rigor, Carson empowers kids to learn faster, master life skills, and believe in themselves.

> With high standards and high support, I push students beyond what they thought possible by connecting their passions to learning and showing them that Alpha prepares them for the life they want.
> 
>  - Carson Lehmann

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/ALPHA_PICDAY_1271-2-1-1024x876.jpg) 

Derek Kim | Guide
-----------------

Education, AI tools, and user experience design come together in Derek Kim’s work as a Guide at Alpha San Francisco, where he helps students push beyond limits and thrive. A decorated Division I student-athlete at Columbia University, he later earned a master’s in Human-Computer Interaction &amp; Design from UC Irvine. Drawing on his experience as both a teacher and college prep advisor, Derek prepares students to succeed in San Francisco’s center of innovation and in the world beyond.

> I model a genuine passion for learning and pass it on—guiding students to nurture curiosity, embrace challenge, and carry the confidence to pursue ambitious futures.
> 
>  - Derek Kim

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/ALPHA_PICDAY_1282-2-1-1015x1024.jpg) 

Ree Yeakley | Guide
-------------------

Ree Yeakley is excited to begin her second year as a Guide at Alpha. With a background in education, literacy, and child development, she loves helping children discover their strengths and grow in confidence. Last year, her students achieved remarkable academic and personal growth, and she’s eager to continue fostering a joyful, supportive space where every child can thrive.

> I will uphold Alpha’s promise by inspiring every child to aim high, supporting them relentlessly, and creating an environment where they feel safe, capable, and excited to learn.
> 
>  - Ree Yeakley

### Campus

- **Alpha San Francisco (https://alpha.school/san-francisco/)**
  - **Email**: admissions.sanfrancisco@alpha.school
  - **Telephone**: +14152865034
  - **Address**: 3741 Buchanan St, San Francisco, California, 94123, US
  - **Geo**: 37.80457, -122.4339406

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha San Francisco serve?**: Alpha San Francisco is located in the Marina District on Buchanan Street, serving families from neighborhoods across the city such as Pacific Heights, Cow Hollow, Russian Hill, and North Beach, as well as the wider Bay Area—from Berkeley to Hillsborough and beyond. Alpha San Francisco delivers an innovative and personalized education for your children.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We explored many spaces across the Bay Area, and this one stood out. It offered the right blend of flexibility, safety, design potential, and proximity to key hubs like Marina Green Park, the Palace of Fine Arts, and the Muni/Caltrain connections downtown—offering easy access from neighborhoods across San Francisco.
- **How much break time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60–90 minutes of break time and play. Students often explore nearby green spaces like Moscone Park or the Marina Green. Our SF location also takes advantage of proximity to local activties that keep our students moving, like Bechmark Climbing Gym, the Monterey Bay Coastal Trail, and La Petite Baleen Swim School.
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Our San Francisco students are mastering core subjects at their own pace—with no gaps, no burnout, and no unnecessary review.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and choose workshops—from coding machines to performing arts—based on interests. Whether a student lives in Hillsborough or South the Marina District, they’re on a path that fits them perfectly.
- **Is Alpha San Francisco open?**: Yes, Alpha San Francisco is open and enrolling for K–10. Since we launched in Fall 2025, we’ve been actively growing. So, if you’d like to tour the campus or connect with a current family, we’d love to show you around.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in Santa Barbara​
----------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Santa Barbara, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Santa Barbara, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Santa Barbara is open and enrolling.

Join us for an info session at our campus on 27 E Cota St, conveniently located in the heart of downtown Santa Barbara, less than a block from State Street, and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Tasha Arnold](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha Schools because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>   - Dr Tasha Arnold

At Alpha, he fosters joy in learning, academic excellence, and life skills, guiding kids beyond their comfort zones to extraordinary futures with adventure and inspiration.

### FAQs

- **Is Alpha Santa Barbara open?**: Yes, Alpha Santa Barbara is open and enrolling for K-12. Since we launched in Fall 2025, we’ve been actively growing. So, if you’d like to tour the campus or connect with a current family, we’d love to show you around.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We explored many spaces across Santa Barbara, and this one stood out. It offers the ideal blend of flexibility, safety, design potential, and proximity to key hubs like downtown, the waterfront, and Highway 101—making it easily accessible from every part of the city. Its central location positions Alpha Santa Barbara as the hub for ambitious students from Montecito, Goleta, Ventura, Ojai, and beyond
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Our Santa Barbara students are mastering core subjects at their own pace—with no gaps, no burnout, and no unnecessary review.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and choose workshops—from marine ecology to entrepreneurship. These life skill workshops are essential for preparing students to lead with confidence, think critically, and thrive in the real world.
- **How much time will students spend on computers?**: At Alpha Santa Barbara, students spend about two hours a day on their computers for academics. The rest of the day is filled with life skill workshops, hands-on projects, creative work, time outdoors, and face-to-face collaboration with peers and Guides. We believe technology is a powerful tool for learning, but it’s only one part of a much bigger, well-rounded day.
- **How does Alpha integrate with Santa Barbara’s culture?**: Alpha Santa Barbara is designed to feel like part of the city, not separate from it. Our workshops and projects tap directly into Santa Barbara’s strengths—students will learn entrepreneurship by working with local founders, explore creativity through partnerships with artists and designers, or study marine ecology right on the Channel Islands. We want students to see their city as an extension of their classroom, building real skills while connecting with the creative, entrepreneurial, and environmental spirit that makes Santa Barbara unique.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha Orange County serve?**: Alpha Orange County is located in Foothill Ranch, serving families from Orange County, Mission Viejo, Rancho Santa Margarita, Portola Hills, and the greater South Orange County area. If you live near ZIP codes like 92610, 92630, or 92691, you’re within a short drive of our campus.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We chose Foothill Ranch for its safety, accessibility, and strong family-oriented community. It’s just minutes from the 241 toll road, with quick access for families commuting from Orange County, Mission Viejo, and Irvine. Being near the Foothill Ranch Towne Centre and Whiting Ranch Wilderness Park means students benefit from both convenience and nature.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60–90 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting. We use our outdoor area for biking, games, and movement breaks—and we’re just a few minutes from Whiting Ranch, a beautiful natural space that brings a breath of fresh air to learning
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Our Orange County students are mastering core subjects at their own pace—with no gaps, no burnout, and no unnecessary review.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and choose workshops—from nature inspired science to digital storytelling—based on interests. Whether a student lives in Foothill Ranch, Portola Hills, or Mission Viejo, they’re on a path that fits them perfectly.
- **Is Alpha Orange County open?**: Yes, Alpha Orange County is open and enrolling for K–3. We’d love to meet your family and show you around—come see how we’re changing what school can be!
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Joshua holds a background in Neuroscience and English. Before joining Alpha, he worked as an entertainment critic and spent over a decade tutoring high school and college students in rhetoric and composition.

> I build allyship with each student, serving as both coach and teammate. We tackle challenges side by side, working hard and supporting each other when it gets tough.
> 
>  - Joshua Lezmi

### Campus

- **Alpha Miami (https://alpha.school/miami/)**
  - **Email**: admissions.miami@alpha.school
  - **Telephone**: +17862544288
  - **Address**: 8000 SW 56th St, Miami, Florida, 33155, US

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha Miami serve?**: Alpha Miami is located just off SW 56th Street serving families from Palmetto Bay, Pinecrest, South Miami, High Pines, Coral Gables, Coconut Grove, Brickell, Key Biscayne, Doral, and nearby areas. If you live near any of these ZIP codes 33157, 33156, 33134, 33130, 33131, 33174, 33165, 33173, 33149, among others, Alpha Miami delivers an innovative and personalized education for your children.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We explored many spaces across Miami, and this one stood out. It offered the right blend of flexibility, safety, design potential, and proximity to key hubs like University of Miami, Coral Gables, and the Palmetto Expressway that offers easy access from all Miami neighborhoods.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60–90 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting. Students often explore nearby green spaces like Tropical Park or enjoy movement games and biking in our own outdoor areas. Our Miami location also takes advantage of proximity to destinations like the Miami Zoo, stables in South Miami’s Horse Country, Olympic-size pools at nearby Miami Dade College, Marine Lab, and more! Fresh air and sunshine are built into our day!
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Our Miami students are mastering core subjects at their own pace—with no gaps, no burnout, and no unnecessary review.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and choose workshops—from marine science to digital storytelling—based on interests. Whether a student lives in Fontainebleau or South Miami Heights, they’re on a path that fits them perfectly.
- **Is Alpha Miami open?**: Yes, Alpha Miami is open and enrolling for K–10. Since we launched in Fall 2024, we’ve been actively growing. So, if you’d like to tour the campus or connect with a current family, we’d love to show you around.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in Palm Beach​
-------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Palm Beach, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

Personalized Learning
---------------------

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Palm Beach, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Palm Beach is open and enrolling.

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha Schools because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>   - Dr Tasha Arnold

### Campus

- **Alpha Palm Beach (https://alpha.school/palm-beach/)**
  - **Email**: admissions.westpalmbeach@alpha.school

### FAQs

- **Is Alpha Palm Beach open?**: Yes, Alpha Palm Beach is open and enrolling for K-5. Since we launched in Fall 2025, we’ve been actively growing. So, if you’d like to tour the campus, or connect with a current family, we’d love to show you around.
- **What communities does Alpha Peach Beach serve?**: Alpha Palm Beach is located just off Northlake Blvd–serving families from Palm Beach Gardens, Jupiter and Palm Beach, west to Royal Palm and Wellington, and down to Delray Beach, Boca Raton, and neighboring areas. If you live in Palm Beach County, or nearby Martin or Broward County, Alpha Palm Beach delivers an innovative and personalized education for your children.
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path built with adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Our Palm Beach students are mastering core subjects at their own pace–with no gaps, no burnout, and no unnecessary review.Outside of academics, Guides work 1:1 with students to set goals and choose workshops–from martial arts to public speaking–based on interests. No matter where a student is from, they’re on a path that fits them perfectly.
- **How much time will students spend on computers?**: At Alpha Palm Beach, students spend about two hours a day on their computers for academics. The rest of the day is filled with life skill workshops, hands-on projects, creative work, time outdoors, and face-to-face collaboration with peers and Guides. We believe technology is a powerful tool for learning, but it’s only one part of a much bigger, well-rounded day.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting. Students often explore nearby green spaces like PGA National Park or enjoy movement games and scootering in our own outdoor areas. Fresh air and sunshine are built into our day!
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM. You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in New York​
-----------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha New York, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha New York, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Join us for an info session at our 180 Maiden Lane location, in Lower Manhattan’s Financial District, just steps from the East River waterfront and the iconic South Street Seaport. It’s one block from the Imagination Playground, with Battery Park and the Brooklyn Bridge a short walk away. See firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Tasha Arnold](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Alpha New York
-----------------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>  - Dr. Tasha Arnold

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Liam2.webp) 

Liam Stanton | Lead Teacher, L2 
--------------------------------

Liam Stanton spent a decade teaching in Colombia, China, and Silicon Valley before joining Alpha. He holds a master’s from Harvard in Learning Design, Innovation &amp; Technology, where he focused on the impact of Al in education, and now designs immersive, real-world learning experiences for students.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/B68I7208-867x1024.jpg) 

Emily Lopez | Teacher, Middle School 
-------------------------------------

Emily Lopez is the Director of Experiential Learning at Alpha and is stepping into the role of Middle School Teacher in New York City. She began her work at Alpha as an L1 Teacher and has since led the design of high-impact, real-world learning programs, drawing on a background in international education and teen mentorship in Spain and Honduras. She is passionate about helping students build independence, confidence, and ownership of their learning through hands-on, high-expectation experiences.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Jenna.png) 

Jenna Petrungaro | Teacher, L2
------------------------------

Jenna Petrungaro is a Teacher at Alpha New York City with six years of experience as a secondary math teacher in public schools. She was born and raised on Long Island and is passionate about helping students build confidence, independence, and genuine joy in learning. Outside of school, Jenna is training for the 2026 NYC Marathon and loves exploring new food spots around the city.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/img_0853_720.jpg) 

Nathan Witkin | Teacher, L1
---------------------------

Nathan Witkin is an educator, writer, and researcher with a background in academic philosophy and competitive high school debate. He previously worked as a teaching assistant at Tufts University while completing his master’s in philosophy, and has coached debate for the Dalton School and the Bronx High School of Science. He is excited to awaken students’ passions at Alpha, and to push them toward new heights in their academics and beyond.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/parthvi.png) 

Parthvi Harde | Teacher, L1
---------------------------

Parthvi Harde has a background working in early-stage startups, where she focused on building programs, collaborating across teams, and navigating fast-moving, ambiguous environments. She’s spent over 4 years being a management consultant to scaling startups in the marketing and climate tech fields. She now brings that real-world experience into her work at Alpha, helping students connect learning to problem-solving, creativity, and ownership. Her approach emphasizes curiosity, clear thinking, and collaboration.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Jenna-Klemm-photo-722x1024.jpg) 

Jenna Klemm | Reading Specialist, ll
------------------------------------

Jenna is an experienced educator and reading specialist with a master’s degree in education and reading and is a proud Penn State graduate. She is trained in Orton-Gillingham–aligned literacy instruction and has years of experience supporting young learners as they build strong foundational reading skills through evidence-based practices that prioritize confidence, connection, and growth. For the remainder of the school year, Jenna will serve as the Reading Specialist at Alpha’s New York campus. She is passionate about partnering with families to support children’s literacy development. Outside of school, Jenna enjoys yoga, spending time with her family, and hanging out with her dog, Ollie.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Julianne-Braime-754x1024.png) 

Julianne Braime | Campus Coordinator
------------------------------------

Julianne is a dedicated education professional with a background in student leadership, academic support, and community engagement. She has worked across higher education and student services, designing and supporting initiatives that foster student success and community connection. With an educational background in Marine Biology and a passion for student success, Julianne brings an organized, thoughtful, and student-centered approach to her role as Campus Coordinator. Outside of work, Julianne enjoys crocheting, practicing yoga, and spending time outdoors.

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/01/Nancy-Torvund-1024x819.jpg) 

Nancy Torvund | Director of Admissions
--------------------------------------

Nancy Torvund is a Penn alum, lifelong learner, and Mensa member with a deeply personal relationship to education. A grade-skipper who began college just after turning seventeen, she understands what it means for students to outpace traditional systems. She started her educational career as a public-school teacher in Norway, later serving as a regional teachers’ union leader before leaving when meaningful change proved structurally out of reach. She went on to build an online learning system at a private school, becoming a shareholder and board member overseeing admissions and strategic development. After long believing a return to the U.S. would require something extraordinary, she found that in Alpha, where she brings a global and personal perspective to helping students find environments where they can thrive.

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha serve?**: Alpha serves families across Lower Manhattan, including the Financial District, Tribeca, Battery Park City, the Lower East Side, and Greenwich Village, as well as nearby Chelsea. Thanks to easy ferry access, we also welcome families from Brooklyn neighborhoods such as Brooklyn Heights and Park Slope. In addition, we support families from surrounding areas and boroughs, offering a convenient and innovative option for those seeking personalized education in New York City. If you live near ZIP codes 10005, 10006, 10007, 10038, 10002, 10003, 10011, or 11201, Alpha is here for you.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We chose 180 Maiden Lane because it offers the perfect mix of accessibility and community. It’s close to families in Lower Manhattan and easily reached by ferry for Brooklyn parents. Just as importantly, our partnership with the building’s developer—who shared our enthusiasm for bringing a groundbreaking, personalized education model to New York—made this the ideal home for Alpha’s first NYC campus.
- **How much outdoor time do students get?**: Every school day includes around 60 minutes of unstructured play, weather permitting. Students often head to nearby play spaces like the Imagination Playground, just one block from our campus, for active outdoor play. In addition, we offer a movement-based workshop twice a week—usually on Tuesdays and Thursdays—ensuring kids stay active, energized, and connected to their environment.
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a customized learning path supported by adaptive apps that adjust in real time to their progress. Students master core subjects at their own pace—no gaps, no burnout, no unnecessary repetition. Beyond academics, Teachers work one-on-one with students to set goals and choose workshops based on their interests—from creative storytelling to robotics—so each learner thrives in a way that fits them perfectly.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

Welcome to the Future of Education in Chantilly​
------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Chantilly, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

Personalized Learning
---------------------

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Chantilly, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Chantilly is open and enrolling for the **2025–26 and 2026–27** school years with rolling admission.

Join us for an info session, and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Tasha Arnold](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>  - Dr. Tasha Arnold

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Jeremy Williams](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/jw-headshot-scaled.webp) 

Dr. Jeremy Williams | Dean of Parents of Alpha School in Chantilly
------------------------------------------------------------------

Dr. Jeremy Williams is an education leader and innovator with a track record of reimagining what school can be. Over the past two decades, he has led schools across the United States and internationally, including Montessori, private, and PK–12th grade programs. His leadership has been defined by one constant: creating schools where students thrive, parents feel like true partners, and innovation drives lasting impact.

> I joined Alpha because I believe what we're doing has the potential to redefine how every child in the world learns.
> 
>  - Dr. Jeremy Williams

 ![Best Private Schools - Alpha School - Stephanie Dean](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/S-Dean-headshot-2025.webp) 

Stephanie Dean | Associate Dean of Parents of Alpha School in Chantilly
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Stephanie is a former teacher and education consultant who helped lead two national initiatives to strengthen K–12 systems. Seeing how difficult it is to create change within traditional schools, she was drawn to Alpha’s bold model. Stephanie now partners with parents and guides to launch and strengthen Alpha’s newest campuses.

> Education is not the filling of a pot but the lighting of a fire.
> 
>   - W.B. Yeats

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/FENNER-Headshot.webp) 

Courtney Fenner | Lead Guide
----------------------------

Courtney brings over 22 years of educational experience as a classroom teacher, team leader, school administrator, and education consultant, working with students in K-16 settings across a breadth of private and public schools. She holds a Bachelor’s degree from the University of Virginia, a Master of Fine Arts from Virginia Commonwealth University, and a Master of Arts from Brooklyn College.

> In service to our community, I strive to be honest about my own rocky paths to mastery, my own mistakes with supporting students, and my encounters with productive struggle to become better!
> 
>  - Courtney Fenner

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Liggans-Hubbard-Photo-959x1024.webp) 

Fau Liggans-Hubbard | Guide
---------------------------

Fau is a Chicago native with a background in global education and student advising across five countries. She holds a BA in Anthropology from the University of Notre Dame and a MA in International Relations from Johns Hopkins SAIS. Fau’s passion for empowering learners to grow with confidence, curiosity, and purpose drew her to the Alpha mission. As a Guide, she is excited to bring her global perspective and creativity to help students thrive not only in school but in life beyond it.

> Steve Jobs once said, 'Stay hungry. Stay foolish,' and it has stuck with me since. Never be afraid to try new and hard things, because making mistakes and learning from them is the only path that has ever led to real growth and success.
> 
>  - Fau Liggans-Hubbard

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2025/10/victoria-768x1024.webp) 

Victoria Schoch | Guide
-----------------------

Victoria holds degrees in Early Childhood, Elementary Education, and Learning Design &amp; Tech. She’s a child development mastermind with an extraordinary gift for unlocking each child’s hidden potential and has a proven track record of transforming struggling students into confident, capable learners while mentoring the whole-child. Where others see challenges, she sees opportunity.

> When you plant lettuce, if it does not grow well, you don't blame the lettuce. You look for reasons it is not doing well. It may need fertilizer, or more water, or less sun. You never blame the lettuce.
> 
>  - Thich Nhat Hanh

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Katie-Pond-1-1024x1024.webp) 

Katie Pond | Guide
------------------

With 17+ years in education, Katie Pond brings experience as a Reading Specialist, curriculum designer, and educator. She holds an M.Ed. from the University of Virginia and specializes in Science of Reading practices. Katie is passionate about helping students build confidence, curiosity, and a love of learning.

> I want students to leave each day believing they can tackle hard things. Growth, confidence, and a love of learning are at the center of everything I do.

### Campus

- **Alpha Chantilly (https://alpha.school/chantilly/)**
  - **Email**: admissions.chantilly@alpha.school
  - **Telephone**: +17033487385
  - **Address**: 4550 Walney Road, Chantilly, Virginia, 20151, US
  - **Geo**: 38.8777046, -77.4353615

### FAQs

- **What communities does Alpha Chantilly serve?**: Alpha Chantilly is located just off Walney Road, serving families from Chantilly, Centreville, Fairfax, Herndon, Oak Hill, South Riding, and Great Falls, as well as nearby communities such as McLean, Vienna, Oakton, Reston, Ashburn, Arlington, and Falls Church. If you live near any of these ZIP codes — 20151, 20120, 22033, 22030, 20171, 20170, 20152, 20105, 22124, 22066, 22101, 22182, 20147, 22207, 22046 — Alpha Chantilly delivers an innovative and personalized education for your children.
- **How did you choose the location?**: We chose our Chantilly campus for its welcoming, family-focused environment, thoughtful design potential, and strong sense of safety. It’s close to Washington D.C., the Dulles Expo Center, Route 28, and sought-after neighborhoods like Centreville, Oak Hill, and McLean—perfectly balancing community feel with convenient access for families seeking a premier education experience.
- **How much break time do students get?**: Every school day includes 60–90 minutes of outdoor play, weather permitting. Students enjoy our campus’s secure outdoor learning areas, playgrounds, and movement games, including biking and active exploration. We also take advantage of well-maintained nearby parks and community green spaces for guided activities. At Alpha Chantilly, fresh air, sunshine, and hands-on exploration are built into every day, supporting curiosity, fitness, and fun.
- **How is learning personalized?**: Each Alpha student follows a tailored learning path powered by adaptive apps that respond in real time to their progress. At Alpha Chantilly, students advance through core subjects at their own pace—ensuring mastery without gaps, burnout, or unnecessary review.Guides partner individually with students to set goals and select workshops—from coding and robotics to creative writing and design thinking—aligned with each child’s passions. Whether a student lives in the serene suburbs of Northern Virginia or closer to the energy of downtown Washington D.C., their education is thoughtfully customized to foster curiosity, confidence, and excellence.
- **Is Alpha Chantilly open?**: Alpha Chantilly will open in Fall 2025 and warmly welcome students to our personalized learning programs. Interested parents can attend info sessions and family nights, or have their children experience a “Day in the Life” during upcoming Shadow Days to meet our Guides, tour the campus, and see firsthand how we nurture curiosity, confidence, and academic excellence. For more information about upcoming events, email admissions.chantilly@alpha.school.
- **What's the daily schedule?**: The daily schedule at Alpha runs from 8:15 AM to 4:00 PM. Students arrive for morning drop-off at 8:15–8:30 AM, and the day finishes with afternoon pick-up between 3:30–4:00 PM.You can find more information on what an Alpha day looks like in the Info Packet linked above.

-----------------------------------------------

Personalized Learning
---------------------

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha East Bay, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha East Bay is launching in Fall 2026.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled-1.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>  - Dr. Tasha Arnold

Welcome to the Future of Education in Santa Monica​
---------------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Santa Monica, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

Personalized Learning
---------------------

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Santa Monica, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Santa Monica is launching in Fall 2026.

Join us for an info session, and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled-1.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>  - Dr. Tasha Arnold

Welcome to the Future of Education in Chicago​
----------------------------------------------

 Looking for a private school your child can’t wait to go to each morning? At Alpha Chicago, our mastery-based, AI driven approach allows students to crush their academics in 2 hours. Our classes rank in [ the top 1% nationally](/the-program/#learn). 

Personalized Learning
---------------------

 The rest of the day is spent on [life skills and team-based workshops](/lifeskills-workshops/) that ignite motivation and teach things like leadership, grit, financial literacy &amp; entrepreneurship. 

 At Alpha Chicago, ***kids love school.*** We’re not just preparing students for tests; we’re preparing them for limitless futures. 

Alpha Chicago is launching in Fall 2026.

Join us for an info session, and see firsthand why Alpha is ranked among the best private schools thanks to its groundbreaking learning model.

Meet our Team
-------------

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Tasha-Arnold-Profile-Pic-scaled-1.webp) 

Dr. Tasha Arnold | Head of Schools
----------------------------------

Dr. Tasha Arnold is a dynamic educational leader with extensive experience in American and international schools across the US, Europe, and Asia. She has spent her career transforming schools, implementing innovative learning models, and fostering personalized educational experiences that empower students to reach their highest potential. She has taught at the Elementary, Middle, and High School levels, specializing in IB/AP Sciences and Learning Support across various curriculums (USA, UK, IB, and AP).

> I joined Alpha because I believe in redefining education. Personalization, hands-on learning, and skill development are the pillars of a truly impactful education. Alpha’s approach aligns with my vision of ensuring every child thrives academically, socially, and emotionally in a way that is uniquely suited to them.
> 
>  - Dr. Tasha Arnold

Joanna Sanner, M.A. | Guide
---------------------------

Joanna Sanner is an experienced Pre-K through 8th-grade educator with a decade of service across general, special, and international education settings, holding a B.A., two M.A.’s, and is currently pursuing a Ph.D in Education Policy, Leadership and Management. Most recently, she spent 4 years in Rwanda, Africa, where she leveraged her expertise to help re-open a preschool that had closed during the COVID-19 pandemic. As a certified Time to Teach trainer, Joanna specializes in maximizing student engagement utilizing Gardner’s Theory of Multiple Intelligences. She is passionate about inspiring every student at Alpha to become a lifelong learner.

> Tell me and I forget. Teach me and I remember. Involve me and I learn.
> 
>  - Xun Kuang

 ![](https://alpha.school/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Jenna-York.webp) 

Jenna York | Campus Coordinator
-------------------------------

Jenna brings over a decade of experience in elementary and middle school education to support both students and staff. She thrives on creating organized and efficient systems that help the school day run smoothly and allow great learning to happen. Known for her strong communication, attention to detail, and ability to bring calm to fast-paced environments, Jenna ensures that everyone on campus feels set up for success. She believes that when a school runs well, students can focus on growing, exploring, and reaching their full potential. Outside of school, she enjoys traveling and spending time with her growing family.

> I will ensure the 2-Hour Learning model runs smoothly each day by building strong systems and clear routines. By supporting both staff and students behind the scenes, I’ll help create the conditions for efficient mastery and meaningful learning experiences.
> 
>  - Jenna York
